const questions = `[
  {
    "code": "Q10",
    "type": "BSP",
    "isRequired": true,
    "commit": "true",
    "name": "Reason for end of working relationship",
    "options": [
      {
        "value": "Budget issue",
        "text": "Budget issue"
      },
      {
        "value": "Performance issue",
        "text": "Performance issue"
      },
      {
        "value": "Communication issue",
        "text": "Communication issue"
      },
      {
        "value": "Personal issue",
        "text": "Personal issue"
      },
      {
        "value": "Organizational issue",
        "text": "Organizational issue"
      },
      {
        "value": "Other issue",
        "text": "Other issue"
      }
    ],
    "page": {
      "isJumpToPage": true,
      "pageNumber": 10
    }
  }
]`;

const questionsJSON = JSON.parse(questions);

const questionsArray = questionsJSON.map((question) => {
  const { value, text, isRequired, commit, name, options, page } = question;

  return {
    value,
    text,
    isRequired,
    commit,
    name,
    options,
    page: {
      isJumpToPage: page.isJumpToPage,
      pageNumber: page.pageNumber,
    },
  };
});

export { questionsArray };

3. Were the course materials and delivery methods easy to understand and use?
4. Were the instructors knowledgeable and able to explain complex topics in an accessible way?
5. Did you feel that the course duration was appropriate, or was it too long or too short?
6. Were the learning objectives and outcomes clearly communicated?
7. Did you have enough opportunities to provide feedback and ask questions during the course?
8. Based on your experience, would you recommend this course to others?

The answer options for multiple choice questions are "Yes" and "No" and for rating questions are "Always", "Most of the time", "Sometimes", "Rarely", and "Never".

3. Do you feel that the current benefits package is sufficient to meet your needs?

5. Do you think that the current benefits package is inclusive and caters to all employees, regardless of their age, gender, or disability status?
6. Have you ever felt that the benefits offered by the company are not inclusive or do not cater to your specific needs?
7. In terms of benefits, do you feel that the company values its employees and prioritizes their well-being?
8. How often do you review the benefits package to ensure that it still meets your needs and preferences?
9. Do you think that the company should invest more in its benefits package to attract and retain top talent?

    "required": true,
    "multiple": false

const questionsJSON = JSON.parse(questions);

const questionsArray = questionsJSON.map((question) => {
  return {
    code: question.code,
    text: question.text,
    image: question.image,
    options: question.options.map((option) => {
      return {
        text: option.text,
        image: option.image,
        value: option.value
      };
    }),
    required: question.required,
    multiple: question.multiple
  };
});

export { questionsArray };

[LLM ANSWER]
 Sure, I can help you generate a questionnaire on the topic of Employee Potential. Here are 10 questions that can be used to assess an employee's potential:

1. How would you describe your level of motivation to learn new skills and take on new responsibilities?
2. Do you feel that you are able to work to the best of your abilities, or do you feel limited by your current role or work environment?
3. How do you feel about receiving feedback and using it to improve your performance?
4. Can you give examples of how you have demonstrated leadership skills in the workplace?
5. How do you assess the needs of your team and make sure that they have the resources they need to be successful?
6. How do you prioritize tasks and projects, and how do you balance the needs of different stakeholders?
7. Can you describe a time when you had to think creatively to solve a problem, and how you went about it?
8. How do you build relationships with colleagues and stakeholders, and how do you maintain those relationships over time?
9. How do you handle stress and pressure, and how do you maintain a positive attitude in the face of challenges?
10. Can you give examples of how you have been able to influence others and bring them along to a new way of thinking?

I hope this questionnaire will be helpful in assessing employee potential! Let me know if you need anything else.

Generate me a questionnaire on Employee Potential with 10 questions

This is a JSON object that represents a questionnaire about leadership skills. The questionnaire has 10 questions, each with a unique code, display order, and type (3 indicates that the answer is a rating on a scale). For each question, there are also up to 4 possible answers, represented as an object with an `ANSWER` property.

Here is a summary of the questionnaire:

- Question 1: How would you describe your level of motivation to learn new skills and take on new responsibilities?
  - Very motivated
  - Somewhat motivated
  - Not very motivated
  - Not at all motivated
- Question 2: Do you feel that you are able to work to the best of your abilities, or do you feel limited by your current role or work environment?
  - Yes, I feel that I am able to work to the best of my abilities
  - No, I feel limited by my current role or work environment
- Question 3: How do you feel about receiving feedback and using it to improve your performance?
  - I enjoy receiving feedback and use it to improve my performance
  - I do not like receiving feedback and do not use it to improve my performance
- Question 4: Can you give examples of how you have demonstrated leadership skills in the workplace?
  - Yes, I have demonstrated leadership skills in the workplace
  - No, I have not demonstrated leadership skills in the workplace
- Question 5: How do you assess the needs of your team and make sure that they have the resources they need to be successful?
  - I assess the needs of my team and make sure that they have the resources they need to be successful
  - I do not assess the needs of my team and make sure that they have the resources they need to be successful
- Question 6: How do you prioritize tasks and projects, and how do you balance the needs of different stakeholders?
  - I prioritize tasks and projects and balance the needs of different stakeholders effectively
  - I do not prioritize tasks and projects and balance the needs of different stakeholders effectively
- Question 7: Can you describe a time when you had to think creatively to solve a problem, and how you went about it?
  - Yes, I can describe a time when I had to think creatively to solve a problem
  - No, I cannot describe a time when I had to think creatively to solve a problem
- Question 8: How do you build relationships with colleagues and how do you maintain these relationships?
  - I build and maintain relationships with colleagues effectively
  - I do not build and maintain relationships with colleagues effectively
- Question 9: How do you communicate with colleagues and how do you handle conflicts?
  - I communicate with colleagues effectively and handle conflicts in a constructive way
  - I do not communicate with colleagues effectively and do not handle conflicts in a constructive way
- Question 10: How do you handle stress and pressure, and how do you take care of yourself?
  - I handle stress and pressure effectively and take care of myself
  - I do not handle stress and pressure effectively and do not take care of myself

3. Have you ever received a recognition or reward that made you feel unappreciated? If yes, please describe the situation.
4. In your opinion, what is the most effective way to reward an employee's good performance?
5. How often do you think recognition and rewards should be given to employees? Please specify.
6. Do you think that recognition and rewards can be automated, or do they need to be personalized? Please explain your answer.
7. In your opinion, what is the most important factor in recognizing and rewarding an employee: the method or the frequency?

| Question | Answer |
| --- | --- |

| 4. In your opinion, what is the most effective way to reward an employee's good performance? | Open |
| 5. How often do you think recognition and rewards should be given to employees? | Frequency |
| 6. Do you think that recognition and rewards can be automated, or do they need to be personalized? | Yes/No, Open |
| 7. In your opinion, what is the most important factor in recognizing and rewarding an employee: the method or the frequency? | Method/Frequency |

6. Can you think of any ways in which the workplace environment could be made more accessible and user-friendly for people with different abilities and needs?
